The `public contributions` by users in Singapore on `2023/12/19 2:28 AM UTC`. This list contains users from `Singapore` and cities`Singapore` and cities.

There are `138 countries` and `674 cities` can be found [here](https://github.com/PushoDev/top-github-users).

There are `930 users`  in Singapore. You need at least `60 followers` to be on this list.

## üì¶ Third party

- [@octokit/graphql](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@octokit/graphql) - Send GraphQL requests to GitHub API.
- [fs-extra](https://www.npmjs.com/package/fs-extra) - Creating directories and files.
- [simple-git](https://www.npmjs.com/package/simple-git) - Handling Git commands.
